 India has received a unique gift from Britain on the occasion of Independence Day
 darasal, britain ne bharat se chori kar le jaai gai puratathvik mahatv kii ek kaansya pratimaa lautaa di he
 This bronze statue is of Lord Buddha which was stolen from a museum in Nalanda in Bihar some 60 years ago
 pitiai kii report ke mutabik buddha pratimaa 12veen sadi kii he
 During the Independence Day celebrations in London, the London Metropolitan Police returned it to India
 kya he murti kii khaasiyat?chaandi kii kalamkaari vaali kaansya murti 1961 main nalanda main bhartiya puraatatv surveykshan santhaan ke ek sangrahalay se churaai gai 14 murtiyon main ek he
 It passed through various hands for years before being brought up for auction in London

 security eps banane vaali sibar security company Sophos dwaara ek likhe gaye ek blog post ke baad google ne apane play store se 22 eps ko delit kar diya he
 These apps were dangerous like a computer or mobile virus
 inamen ek balldor banaaya gaya tha jo vigyaapan ke jariye frod karne main madad karata tha
 These 22 had been downloaded a total of 20 million times before they were deleted
 Sophos ne apni jaanch main paaya ki ye eps Andr and Clickr-ad network se linkd the
 The security company wrote that they are a well-organized malware that can cause deep damage to users and the entire Android ecosystem
 kyonki ye eps phek clic ke jariye vigyaapan network kaa acha khaas revenue dete hai
 Sophos has explained in his blog how these apps can harm people's phones
 company ne bataaya ki ye eps phone kii bydaree ko khatm kar dete hai or ye data overej kaa bhi kaaran ban sakate hai kyonki ye eps lagaataar chal rahe hote hai or becoground main sarwar se communicket kar rahe hote hai
 Apart from this, since the device is completely under C2 server control, any dangerous module can be installed on the phone on the instruction of the server
 yani kul milakar ye 22 eps aapke phone par nahin hone chahie
 Currently, after Sophos report, Google has removed these apps from the Play Store
 haalanki ye saaf nahin ki kya in eps ko logon ke smartfones se hataaya gaya he yaa nahin
 If the apps are downloaded from the Play Store and users are connected to the Internet, then Google can delete the installed apps directly from people's phones
 ye pehali dfa nahin he jab popular eps kaa naam clic frod main aayaa he
 Earlier too many popular apps like Clean Master's name also came up in a similar case
 yahaan dekhen un 22 eps kii list jo aapke phone main nahin hone chahie--- Sparkle flashlight-- Snake Attack-- Math Solver-- shapesorter-- Tak a Trip-- Magnifeye-- Join Up-- Zombie Killer-- Space Rocket-- Neon Pong-- Just Flashlight-- Table Soccer-- Cliff Diver-- Box Stack-- Jelly Slice-- AK Blackjack-- Color Tiles-- Animal Match-- Roulette Mania-- hexafall-- hexablocks-- pairzapye un eps kii list hai jinhen apane phone se hataa dena hi behatar hoga
